3. Sentence: 他們只是碰上了鐵石心腸的法官、無能的律師、警察的誣告，而成為受害者，再不然就是運氣實在太壞了。
   Translation: They just ran into a heartless judge, an incompetent lawyer, false accusations by the police, and became victims, or else they were really unlucky.

Translation: Even though they swear on the Bible, they are hypocritical, just like TV evangelists who talk nonsense.

Grammar structure: This sentence uses the structure "儘管...但卻...", which means "even though...but...". It is used to express a contrast between two situations.

Important words:
- 儘管 (gan1 guan3): even though
- 手按《聖經》宣誓 (shou3 an4 "sheng4 jing1" xuan1 shi4): swear on the Bible

- 信口開河 (xin4 kou3 kai1 he2): talk nonsense

2. 大多數囚犯都不是什麼好人，無論對自己或對別人，都沒什麼好處，他們最大的不幸，就是被生到這世上來。

Translation: Most prisoners are not good people, whether for themselves or for others, there is no benefit, their biggest misfortune is being born into this world.

Grammar structure: This sentence uses the structure "無論...都...", which means "no matter...all...". It is used to express that no matter what the condition is, the result is the same.

Important words:

- 不幸 (bu4 xing4): misfortune
- 世上 (shi4 shang4): world1. 我在肖申克的那些年中，儘管許多人告訴我他們是無辜的，但我相信其中真正無辜的人不超過十個。

   Translation: The prosecution authorities believe that the evidence in this case is almost irrefutable.

1. "你那天晚上帶着你的點三八口徑手槍嗎？"

Translation: "Did you bring your .38 caliber handgun that night?"

Grammar Structure: The sentence starts with "你" (you), followed by "那天晚上" (that night), "帶着" (bring), "你的" (your), "點三八口徑手槍" (.38 caliber handgun), and ends with "嗎" which is a question particle.

Important Words:
- 你 (you) [nei5]
- 那天晚上 (that night) [naa6 tin1 maan5 seung6]
- 帶着 (bring) [daai3 ze2]
- 點三八口徑手槍 (.38 caliber handgun) [dim2 saam1 baat3 hau2 ging6 sau2 coeng1]
- 嗎 (question particle) [maa3]

2. "沒有，我已經説過了——"

Translation: "No, I've already said ——"

Grammar Structure: The sentence starts with "沒有" (no), followed by "我" (I), "已經" (already), "説過了" (said), and ends with "——" which is a punctuation mark for an unfinished sentence.

Important Words:
- 沒有 (no) [mut6 jau5]
- 我 (I) [ngo5]
- 已經 (already) [ji5 ging1]
- 説過了 (said) [syut3 gwo3 liu5]

3. "哦！對了！”檢察官諷刺地微笑道，“你把它扔進河裏了，是嗎？在九月九日的下午，扔進皇家河中。”

Translation: "Oh! Right!” The prosecutor sarcastically smiled, “You threw it into the river, didn't you? In the afternoon of September 9th, threw it into the Royal River."

Grammar Structure: This sentence is a bit complex as it contains dialogue and narrative. It starts with an exclamation "哦！對了！” (Oh! Right!), then introduces the speaker "檢察官" (prosecutor), followed by the action "諷刺地微笑道" (sarcastically smiled), then another dialogue "你把它扔進河裏了，是嗎？" (You threw it into the river, didn't you?), and ends with a time and place "在九月九日的下午，扔進皇家河中" (In the afternoon of September 9th, threw it into the Royal River).

Important Words:
- 哦！對了！(Oh! Right!) [o4! dung6 liu5!]
- 檢察官 (prosecutor) [gim2 caat3 gun1]
- 諷刺地微笑道 (sarcastically smiled) [fung6 ci3 dei6 mei4 siu3 dou6]
- 你把它扔進河裏了，是嗎？(You threw it into the river, didn't you?) [nei5 baa2 keoi1 wing6 zeon3 ho4 lei5 liu5, si6 maa3?]
- 在九月九日的下午，扔進皇家河中 (In the afternoon of September 9th, threw it into the Royal River) [zoi6 gau2 jyut6 gau2 jat6 dik1 haa6 ng5, wing6 zeon3 wong4 gaa1 ho4 zung1]1. Sentence: “是的，先生。”
Translation: "Yes, sir."
Grammar Structure: This sentence is a simple declarative sentence with the subject implied (it). "是的" is an affirmative response, equivalent to "yes" in English. "先生" is a formal address for a man, similar to "sir" in English.
Important Words: 
- 是的 (si6 dik1): yes
- 先生 (sin1 sang1): sir

2. Sentence: “在謀殺案發生的前一天。”
Translation: "The day before the murder case happened."
Grammar Structure: This sentence is a prepositional phrase. "在" introduces the time when something happens. "謀殺案" is the object of the sentence, and "發生的前一天" describes when this event happened.
Important Words:
- 在 (zoi6): at/in/on
- 謀殺案 (mau4 saat3 on3): murder case
- 發生 (faat3 sang1): happen
- 前一天 (cin4 jat1 tin1): the day before

3. Sentence: “是的，先生。”
Translation: "Yes, sir."
(Refer to the first sentence for grammar structure and important words)

4. Sentence: “真是太巧了，不是嗎？”
Translation: "It's really a coincidence, isn't it?"
Grammar Structure: This sentence is a rhetorical question. "真是太巧了" is an exclamatory phrase expressing surprise or disbelief. "不是嗎" is a tag question used to seek agreement or confirmation.
Important Words:
- 真是 (zan1 si6): really
- 太巧了 (taai3 haau2 liu5): too coincidental
- 不是嗎 (bat1 si6 maa3): isn't it

5. Sentence: “這無所謂巧不巧合，是事實罷了。”
Translation: "Whether it's a coincidence or not, it's just a fact."
Grammar Structure: This sentence is a complex sentence. "這無所謂巧不巧合" is the first clause expressing indifference to whether something is a coincidence or not. "是事實罷了" is the second clause stating that it's just a fact.
Important Words:
- 這 (ze2): this
- 無所謂 (mou4 so2 wai6): doesn't matter
- 巧不巧合 (haau2 bat1 haau2 hap6): whether it's a coincidence or not
- 是事實 (si6 si6 sat6): it's a fact
- 罷了 (baa6 liu5): just/only1. "我相信你已經聽過明徹警官的證詞了吧？"

   Translation: Can buy those guys, but also can't coax them with sweet words.

The first clause "能收買那些傢伙" uses the modal verb "能" (can) to express ability, followed by the verb "收買" (to buy), and the object "那些傢伙" (those guys). The second clause "無法用甜言蜜語哄他們" uses "無法" (cannot) to express inability, followed by the phrase "用甜言蜜語" (with sweet words) to describe the method, and the verb "哄" (to coax) with the object "他們" (them).

   - 他們 (taa1 bun2): they, them

   - Important Words: 事後 (afterwards) - si6 hau6, 你 (you) - nei5, 得 (have to) - dak1, 用 (use) - jung6, 鐵鍬 (iron hoe) - tit3 ce4, 或 (or) - waak6, 鑽子 (drill) - zyun3 zi2, 才 (only then) - coi4, 有辦法 (have a way) - jau5 baan6 faat3, 把 (to) - baa2, 他的 (his) - keoi5 dik1, 下巴 (jaw) - haa6 baa1, 撬開 (pry open) - koek3 hoi1Sentence 1: 結果，一九四八年二月的那個晚上，博格斯沒敢放任何東西到安迪嘴巴里。
Translation: As a result, on that night in February 1948, Bogs didn't dare to put anything into Andy's mouth.
Grammar Structure: Subject + Time + Negative Verb + Object + Place
Important Words:
- 結果 (jit6 gwo2): result
- 一九四八年二月 (jat1 gau2 sei3 baat3 nin4 ji6 jyut6): February 1948
- 那個晚上 (naa5 go3 maan5 seung6): that night
- 博格斯 (bok3 gaak3 si1): Bogs (a name)
- 沒敢 (mut6 gam2): didn't dare
- 放任何東西 (fong3 yam6 ho4 dung1 sai1): put anything
- 到安迪嘴巴里 (dou3 on1 dik1 zeui2 baa1 lei5): into Andy's mouth

Sentence 2: 盧斯特也沒有，就我所知，以後也沒有任何人敢這麼做。
Translation: Rooster also didn't, as far as I know, no one dared to do so afterwards.
Grammar Structure: Subject + Negative Verb + Relative Clause + Future Negative Verb + Object
Important Words:
- 盧斯特 (lou4 si1 dak6): Rooster (a name)
- 也沒有 (ya5 mut6 jau5): also didn't
- 就我所知 (jau6 ngo5 so2 zi1): as far as I know
- 以後 (ji5 hau6): afterwards
- 任何人 (yam6 ho4 jan4): anyone
- 敢這麼做 (gam2 ze2 mo1 zou6): dared to do so

Sentence 3: 他們三個人結結實實把安迪打了一頓，差那麼一點點就把他打死。
Translation: The three of them beat Andy up seriously, they were just a little bit away from beating him to death.

- 打死 (daa2 sei2): beat to death

   - Translation: If any prisoner working on the roof dares to act rashly,
   - Grammar: This is a conditional sentence, starting with "要是" (if), followed by the subject "哪個在屋頂上工作的囚犯" (any prisoner working on the roof), and ending with the verb "敢" (dare) and the action "輕舉妄動" (act rashly).
   - Key words:
     - 要是 (jyu1 si6): if
     - 哪個 (naa4 go3): which one, any
     - 屋頂 (uk1 deng2): roof
     - 工作 (gung1 zok3): work
     - 囚犯 (cau4 faan6): prisoner
     - 敢 (gam2): dare
     - 輕舉妄動 (hing1 geoi2 mong6 dung6): act rashly

2. 只消四秒鐘，就會被點四五口徑的機關槍掃成馬蜂窩，
   - Translation: In just four seconds, they would be riddled with bullets from a .45 caliber machine gun,
   - Grammar: This sentence uses the structure "只消...就會" (only takes...then will), indicating a quick consequence. The subject is implied from the previous sentence.
   - Key words:
     - 只消 (zi2 siu1): only takes
     - 秒鐘 (miu5 zung1): second (time)
     - 點 (dim2): hit, point
     - 口徑 (hau2 ging6): caliber
     - 機關槍 (gei1 gwaan1 coeng4): machine gun
     - 掃成 (sou3 sing4): sweep into, riddled with
     - 馬蜂窩 (maa5 fung1 wo1): beehive, here it means riddled with holes

3. 所以那些警衞都很悠閒地坐在那裏；
   - Translation: Therefore, those guards sit there leisurely;

   - Translation: If there are still a few cans of beer buried in the crushed ice to drink, it would simply be as blissful as immortals.

     - 簡直 (gaan2 zik6): simply

   Translation: In 1950, the warden was a northerner named George Dunahy, he got a degree in prison administration.
   Grammar Structure: SVO structure. The subject is "一九五〇年的時候，典獄長是個叫喬治·鄧納海的北方佬", the verb is "拿了", and the object is "個獄政學的學位".

   - 獄政學 (juk6 zing3 hok6): prison administrationSentence 1: 就我所知，除了任命他的那些人之外，沒有人喜歡他。
Translation: As far as I know, apart from those who appointed him, no one likes him.
Grammar Structure: This sentence is a complex sentence with two clauses. The first clause "就我所知" is an adverbial clause of concession, and the second clause "除了任命他的那些人之外，沒有人喜歡他" is the main clause.
Important Words:
- 就我所知 (jau4 ngo5 so2 zi1): as far as I know
- 除了 (ceoi4 leoi5): except for
- 任命 (jam6 ming6): appoint
- 那些 (naa6 se1): those
- 人 (jan4): people
- 喜歡 (hei2 fun2): like
- 他 (taa1): he/him

Sentence 2: 我聽説他只對三件事有興趣：第一是收集統計資料來編他的書（這本書後來由一家叫“粉輕鬆”的小出版社出版，很可能是他自費出版的），其次是關心每年九月哪個球隊贏得監獄棒球聯誼賽冠軍，第三是推動緬因州通過死刑法。
Translation: I heard that he is only interested in three things: the first is to collect statistical data to compile his book (this book was later published by a small publishing house called "Relaxing Powder", it is very likely that he self-published), the second is to care about which team wins the prison baseball league championship every September, and the third is to promote the death penalty law in Maine.
Grammar Structure: This sentence is a compound-complex sentence with multiple clauses. The main clause is "我聽説他只對三件事有興趣", and the following are coordinate clauses listing the three things he is interested in.
Important Words:
- 我聽説 (ngo5 ting1 syut3): I heard
- 只對 (zi2 deoi3): only towards

- 編 (pin1): compile
- 書 (syu1): book

- 自費出版 (zi6 fai3 ceot1 baan2): self-publish
- 關心 (gwaan1 sam1): care about
- 每年 (mui5 nin4): every year
- 九月 (gau2 jyut6): September
- 球隊 (kau4 deoi6): team
- 贏得 (jeng4 dak1): win
- 監獄棒球聯誼賽冠軍 (gaam1 juk6 paang4 kau4 lyun4 ji4 coi3 gun3 gwan1): prison baseball league championship
- 推動 (teoi1 dung6): promote

Translation: The most important thing is, I want to tell him that the situation is bad enough, don't make things worse than they are now.

Grammar Structure: This sentence is a complex sentence with multiple clauses. It starts with an independent clause "最重要的是" (The most important thing is), followed by a dependent clause "我想告訴他" (I want to tell him). Then, there are two more dependent clauses "情況已經夠糟了" (the situation is bad enough) and "不要把事情弄得比現在更糟" (don't make things worse than they are now).

Important Words:
- 最重要 (zui4 zhong4 yao4): most important
- 告訴 (gao4 su4): tell
- 情況 (qing2 kuang4): situation
- 已經 (yi3 jing1): already
- 糟 (zao1): bad
- 不要 (bu4 yao4): don't
- 事情 (shi4 qing2): things
- 弄得 (nong4 de2): make
- 現在 (xian4 zai4): now
- 更糟 (geng4 zao1): worse

Sentence 2: “因為像我們這種人，我們知道在超凡入聖與無惡不作之間還有第三種選擇，這是所有成熟的成年人都會選擇的一條路。”

The sentence ends with two independent clauses: "我是个廉价劳动力" (I was cheap labor) and "这是我们之间的交易" (this was our deal).

   Translation: He helped Tommy review the subjects he studied in high school (not many), and then pass the equivalency exam.

3. 同時他也指導湯米如何利用函授課程，把以前不及格或沒有修過的科目修完。
   Translation: At the same time, he also guided Tommy on how to use correspondence courses to complete the subjects he had previously failed or not studied.
   Grammar Structure: The sentence begins with a time adverbial clause (同時, "At the same time") and contains two clauses connected by comma. The first clause describes an action (他也指導湯米如何利用函授課程, "he also guided Tommy on how to use correspondence courses") and the second clause describes the result (把以前不及格或沒有修過的科目修完, "to complete the subjects he had previously failed or not studied").
   Vocabulary:
   - 同時 (tóngshí): at the same time
   - 指導 (zhǐdǎo): to guide
   - 如何 (rúhé): how
   - 利用 (lìyòng): to use

Grammar structure: This sentence is a complex sentence with three clauses. The first clause "湯米給的這把鑰匙正好可以打開牢籠" is the main clause, and the other two "放出希望的老虎" and "在他腦中咆哮着" are subordinate clauses.

- 正好 (zing3 hou2): just, exactly

Translation: Oh God, when I was finally able to get out of jail and leave that cell, I really felt grateful.

Grammar Structure: This sentence is a complex sentence with two clauses. The first clause "當我終於可以出獄、離開那個牢房時" is a time clause indicating the time when the action in the main clause happened. The main clause "真是覺得謝天謝地" expresses the speaker's feeling at that time.

Important words:
- 老天 (lou5 tin1): God
- 當 (dong1): when
- 終於 (zung1 jyu1): finally
- 可以 (ho2 ji5): can, be able to
- 出獄 (ceot1 juk6): get out of jail
- 離開 (lei4 hoi1): leave
- 那個 (naa5 go3): that
- 牢房 (lou4 fong4): cell
- 真是 (zan1 si6): really
- 覺得 (gok3 dak1): feel
- 謝天謝地 (ze6 tin1 ze6 dei6): thank heaven and earth, feel very grateful

"Solo confinement," Norton said, probably saying it while touching his 30-year commemorative badge, "only given water and bread."

The next part of the sentence is a subordinate clause that provides additional information about Norton's actions (probably saying it while touching his 30-year commemorative badge). The sentence ends with another direct quote ("only given water and bread.").

The main verb (dragged out) comes after the object. The sentence continues with another subject (he) and verb (was shouting), followed by a direct quote ("This is my life, my life, don't you understand? My life--").

The rest of the sentences follow a similar pattern and can be broken down in the same way.Sentence 1: 惟有諾頓可能在一旁幸災樂禍，那個龜兒子，他喜歡監獄裏的人整天灰頭土臉。

Translation: Only Norton might be gloating on the side, that bastard, he likes the people in the prison to be downcast all day.

Grammar Structure: This is a compound-complex sentence. It starts with the subject "諾頓" and the verb "可能" indicating possibility. The phrase "在一旁幸災樂禍" is an adverbial phrase describing the action. The second clause "那個龜兒子" is an appositive providing additional information about the subject. The third clause "他喜歡監獄裏的人整天灰頭土臉" is a complete sentence with its own subject, verb, and object.

Important Words:
- 惟有 (wai4 jau5): only
- 諾頓 (nok6 deon6): Norton
- 可能 (ho2 nang4): might
- 幸災樂禍 (hing3 zoi1 lok6 wo6): gloat
- 龜兒子 (gwai1 ji4 zi2): bastard
- 監獄 (gaam1 juk6): prison
- 灰頭土臉 (fui1 tau4 tou2 min6): downcast

Sentence 2: 但是安迪的心情沒有跌到谷底，也許因為反正他原本就不是棒球迷。

Translation: But Andy's mood didn't hit rock bottom, perhaps because after all, he was not a baseball fan.

Grammar Structure: This is a compound sentence. The first clause "安迪的心情沒有跌到谷底" is a negative sentence with the verb "沒有" indicating absence. The second clause "也許因為反正他原本就不是棒球迷" is a complete sentence with its own subject, verb, and object.

Important Words:
- 但是 (daan6 hai6): but
- 安迪 (on1 dik1): Andy
- 心情 (sam1 cing4): mood
- 谷底 (guk1 dai2): rock bottom
- 也許 (jaa5 heoi2): perhaps
- 反正 (faan2 zing3): after all
- 棒球迷 (paang4 kau4 mai4): baseball fan1. 雖然如此，他似乎感染了這種振奮的氣氛，
